   <script>
    var magImage = document.querySelector('.atkGlobalSiteNav__menu--image img');
   var mobileMagImage = document.querySelector('.atkOffsitePanel .atkGlobalSiteNav__menu--image img');
   var magLink = document.querySelector('#global-nav-latest-issue-ci');
   var mobileMagLink = document.querySelector('.atkOffsitePanel  #global-nav-latest-issue-ci');
 
 
   if ( document.querySelector('meta[name=magazine_image]') != null ) {
     magLink.setAttribute('href', magLink.href.concat(document.querySelector('meta[name=magazine_slug]').getAttribute('content')));
     mobileMagLink.setAttribute('href', mobileMagLink.href.concat(document.querySelector('meta[name=magazine_slug]').getAttribute('content')));
     magImage.setAttribute('src', document.querySelector('meta[name=magazine_image]').getAttribute('content'));
     mobileMagImage.setAttribute('src', document.querySelector('meta[name=magazine_image]').getAttribute('content'));
     magImage.classList.remove('hidden');
     mobileMagImage.classList.remove('hidden');
   }
   </script>

           Recipe

          <h1 class="ts-lg@tablet-only ts-xx-lg@desktop mb-md@mobile-only mb-sm@tablet">
           <a href="https://www.cooksillustrated.com/recipes/9897-grilled-cauliflower">
            Grilled Cauliflower
           </a>
          </h1>
         </div>
         <a class="ts-md@mobile-only ts-x-sm@tablet-only ts-md@desktop t-alt tc-dk-brown lh-x-lg lh-xx-lg@tablet lh-x-lg@desktop bb-s-sm bc-dk-tan b-n@tablet pb-x-lg@mobile-only mb-sm@mobile-only mb-lg@tablet-only" href="https://www.cooksillustrated.com/recipes/9897-grilled-cauliflower">
          Char, caramelization, and smoke bring new dimension to this versatile vegetable. We first microwaved the cauliflower until it was cooked through and then briefly grilled it to pick up color and flavor. To ensure that it held up on the grill without falling through the grate and to provide sufficient surface area for browning, we cut the head into wedges.
